## 5. Cross-run comparison — all metrics in one table

Each row is one model run / split for which we have predictions vs. actuals saved. **R²** is the squared Pearson correlation, RMSE/MAE are on the original SOC scale (g/kg), RPIQ = (Q3 − Q1) / RMSE.

> **Bias sign convention.** The `Bias` column here is `mean(prediction − actual)` (positive = model over-predicts SOC). Some pre-stored `analysis_results.pkl` files instead define `bias = mean(actual − prediction)`; in §3 the “stored” line uses that opposite sign. The two have identical magnitude.

| Source | Split | n | R² | RMSE | MAE | RPIQ | Bias |
|--------|-------|---|----|------|-----|------|------|
| `Weights-ResidualsModels-MappingInference-SOCmapping/Archive/residual_analysis1mil_normalize_composite_l2_v2_TemporalFusionTransformer/analysis_results.pkl` | train_results | 15155 | 0.8659 | 7.5378 | 3.3695 | 1.5522 | -0.3137 |
